style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：江苏省南通市民营企业家，其经营的源景公司与江苏宝泽公司的一起施工合同纠纷案诉讼中败诉。张卫国认为该案败诉系通州区人民法院法官俞妙琴“枉法裁判”所致，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日在本地濠滨论坛发帖，实名举报俞妙琴法官，并留下了自己的姓名、身份证号、手机号、居住地址等信息。此贴点击量暴涨，引起轰动。发帖一个月后，通州区人民法院向公安机关报警。警方以张卫国涉嫌寻衅滋事罪予以刑拘，随后逮捕。检察院提起公诉，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，江苏省南通市海门区人民法院公开审理张卫国被“寻衅滋事”罪。这是第三次公开开庭审理，尚未判决。张卫国利用网络举报法官俞妙琴枉法裁判完全符合《宪法》第<span lang="EN-US">35</span>、<span lang="EN-US">41</span>条规定。被举报人利用公权力对张卫国进行打击报复，与依法治国精神、保护民营企业家政策相悖。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张文斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">原籍山东、原定今年大学毕业。因<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日在微信实名公开发布“习近平下课”、“共产党下课”视频后，其微信被封杀，后又遭强迫失踪，目前处于失联状态。此前他曾因言获罪被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天。张文斌说，自己挺身而出，武汉肺炎疫情是导火索。而这段矛头指向习近平的视频使他又遭遇了强迫失踪。目前没有进一步的信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张文涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西南昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份，南昌市西湖区公安分局与东湖区公安分局联合，成立了迫害法轮功学员的专案组。他们通过摄像头查找后进行抓捕、抄家，分别于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日逐一抓捕了张莉、江兰英、张文涛、胡水英、陈宝芝。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，江西省南昌市西湖区法院判法轮功学员张文涛<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US"> 2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张五洲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">人权捍卫者、湖北籍、家住广东清远市。张五洲是被关进广州白云区看守所死亡的张六毛的姐姐。张五洲为了给弟弟的不明死亡讨回公道受到打压，开始关注公益和参与一些民主、人权活动。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，广州女律师孙世华在广州荔湾区华林派出所办案时，受到该所民警殴打并遭脱衣检查侮辱。随行的张五洲和梁颂基作为目击者，在网上公开为孙世华作证。广州警方为此报复，以“寻衅滋事罪”抓捕了张五洲和梁颂基。后梁颂基被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半和张五洲<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。张五洲女士于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日当天，前往广州著名风景区白云山，在山上栏杆上打出横幅，上书“勿忘六世，撤回恶法”、“女律师被殴目击证人”等字样，以此纪念<span lang="EN-US">31</span>年前的六四事件，以及反对中共两会刚刚通过的香港国安法的实施。张五洲把该活动拍照及视频发微信朋友圈和其它平台发布后，翌日（<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日）下午<span lang="EN-US">14</span>时<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分，广东清远市公安局清城区分局石角派出所以张五洲“涉嫌扰乱公共秩序”为由将其清远市家中传唤带走，随后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日来警方又来抄家。后狱中遭受极其残暴的酷刑虐待。张五洲案于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在清远市清城区法院开庭，未当庭宣判。张五洲在被法院开庭<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月后宣判，以寻衅滋事罪、妨碍公务罪被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，合并执行<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张希明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市东丽区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日上午九点三十分，天津市东丽区分局警察、国保大队便衣、军粮城派出所警察共十几个人，闯入张希明家中，强行非法抄家，并抓捕了张希明与他母亲刘玉红。当天下午五点，警察把刘玉红放回家，当晚把张希明关押到东丽区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，军粮城派出所两个警察给刘玉红送来张希明被刑事拘留的通知书。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底被开庭，后获悉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁左右，大连市中山区人，原中山区青云小学教师，法轮功学员，良心犯。因信仰法轮功并起诉江泽民，曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，被送洗脑班<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日在学校上班时间又被大连市国保与民主广场派出所警方联合绑架抓走，家被查抄，电脑及相关法轮功资料等均被搜走。其丈夫孙俊区派出所问询，已被扣押，后得知夫妇二人均被关押在大连市姚家看守所羁押。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其被大连中山区检察院以涉嫌“邪教罪”正式批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年被大连市中山区法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密判处<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月。其不服提起上诉，大连市中级法院未经二审即对她维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底，张霞被送往辽宁省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张小麦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">原名陈煜，浙江临海市基督徒。张小麦</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">(</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈煜）因在开设网上书店“小麦书房”销售基督教书籍</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">,</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月被捕</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">,</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">在张小麦于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月被中共当局以「网上销售非法境外宗教出版物」被捕后，公安部曾通报全国，要求各地国保根据从「小麦书房」搜到的发货订单接触收货人，就其购买书籍的取向和「当地非法宗教活动的情况」进行取证，有上万人被问询。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">27</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日一审判决，以非法经营罪判</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span><span minor-fareast;">年有期徒刑。并处以罚金</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万，所扣押</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12864</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本书予以销毁。判决书同时裁定，被告除了被罚</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元外，还须追缴售书违法所得的</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元上缴国库，无法追缴的，由被告退赔，并须予判决生效后十天内缴纳。这是对传播基督教的基督徒的赤裸裸的镇压。刑期至：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2026</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张小平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洛阳维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>号，洛阳政府为了修建西环路，在程序不合法的情况下，对张小平家宅基地上的房屋进行了强拆，张小平也因此被逼自学法律，走上了依法维权抗争之路。张小平通过信息公开、行政诉讼等法律途径获取了一些关于修建道路的政府信息，通过对这些信息的分析，发现了前洛阳市市长郭洪昌、李柳身违法修建西环路造成至少<span lang="EN-US">1</span>亿元国有资产流失的事实。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，张小平就这一事实，实名向驻河南中央第一巡视组<span lang="EN-US">65</span>号邮寄了一封《举报信》，此信查询单显示<span lang="EN-US">3.28</span>日已经妥投。巡视组不但没有保护张小平举报人的身份，此举更是将张小平暴露在被举报人的眼皮之下，被打击报复也是迟早之事； 因为举报的事情，张小平接到过威胁电话。关于泄漏举报人信息的问题，张小平通过新浪微博发声质疑，并要求相关部门查处。其最后一个博文发于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，结果，违法人员没得到查处，举报人却被抓了进去。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，洛阳公民张小平疑因举报厅级干部被刑事拘留，其丈夫张智斌行政拘留。原因疑是他们向中央巡视组举报原洛阳市市长郭洪昌、李柳身（正厅级干部）。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，张小平被洛阳公安局南昌路分局（电话<span lang="EN-US">0379-64316110</span>）抓捕；涉嫌罪名是“寻衅滋事”，<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日早被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被批捕。羁押在洛阳看守所。后无进一步信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张小琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆涪陵区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，女。张小琴<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日在涪陵讲法轮功时被构陷，被涪陵区国保警察抓捕、抄家。抄走电脑、打印机、大法书籍等物品，后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，张小琴被批捕。被绑架构陷大半年后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被重庆南川区法院庭审，后悉被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张星姬<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省长春市二道区朝鲜族法轮功学员。千根太、张星姬夫妇在修炼法轮功前，曾在长春市二道区创办食品厂，一九九九年七月中共开始迫害法轮功后，很多法轮功学员进京和平请愿，有的被迫害致流离失所、无家可归。千根太、张星姬夫妇收留几位法轮功学员，被中共发现，后来被迫关闭了食品厂。中共警察上门骚扰不断，千根太、张星姬夫妇不得不将家里的三套房子变卖，被迫流离失所。后遭劳教。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月下旬，千根泰、张星姬夫妇被长春市二道区公安分局和顺街派出所警察抓捕、关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉，千根泰、张星姬夫妇被长春市二道区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张雪春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">微信名海燕，维权人士。于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被沈阳市和平分局以（聚众犹乱社会秩序）罪刑拘，目前关押在沈阳市第一看守所，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日批捕。张雪春家人委托的代理律师向大家征集在北京最高检察院、最高人民法院的目击证人，证明张雪春在按照我国相关法律法规，依法有序向最高人民检察院，最高人民法院，提出司法改革建议过程中，没有任何违法行为，更没有任何犯罪行为以事实，然后走正常法律程序，还当事人以清白，请大家自愿报名，为张雪春出庭作证，证明其当事人无罪。已有上百人目击者报名上庭作证。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张雪莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">甘肃酒泉市瓜州县法轮功学员。此前，张雪莲因信仰真、善、忍，曾被吉林省长春黑嘴子劳教所劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，被无理剥夺工作，并曾被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，在甘肃女子监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，张雪莲，被国保警察抓捕到敦煌看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，在没有通知家人的情况下，敦煌法院去看守所，宣读对张雪莲的判决结果：<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张永宝</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：辽宁省鞍山市人，法轮功信仰者。因信仰、宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日晚在高俊的七岭子家中，张永宝、高俊、、二人被辽阳公安局警察跟踪绑架、构陷，后经辽阳县法院三次庭审，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日二人被一审以犯“邪教罪”分别冤判有期徒刑。其中，高俊被重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其不服已提起上诉。张永宝被冤判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.95pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张玉莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省南阳市法轮功学员，年过七旬。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，张玉莲曾两次被判刑，累计陷冤狱七年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>至<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，河南省南阳市公安局统一行动，在南阳地区开始大面积绑架法轮功学员。两陷冤狱的七旬法轮功学员张玉莲老太再被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，张玉莲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月，勒索罚金五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张玉明：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1955</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，河北遵化市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，遵化多个村镇的数十名法轮功学员几乎同时在凌晨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点多遭到警察的入室抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日张玉明被遵化市法院宣判<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">,</span></b>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">6000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张元华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川泸州市纳溪区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年四十八岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日上午，四川泸州市七名法轮功学员高贤英、董国珍、周明英、张元华、刘忠芬、帅先芳、宋平（男）驱车到泸州市合江县五通镇赶场，被派出所警察抓捕，然后带到合江九支镇派出所审问。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月取保候审。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被四川泸州市合江县法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，处罚金六千。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张展</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代出生，陕西省籍人，上海市浦东新区常驻居民，网络异见人士，公民记者、民主公民。硕士学位，毕业后即在上海谋职工作；因不满中共政府的政治现状，长期在网络平台发布批评“一党专政”、腐败滥权等言论，其做派活跃、内容尖锐而颇具针对性，故而曾多次被上海市警方约谈、传唤及威胁；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年以来，因其在微信等网络平台大量转发香港“反送中”抗议视频及文图资料，尤其是每天自己撰文发声，利用行为艺术等为声援香港举牌，随于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被上海警方传唤，自此失联，后知其被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，其父因受警方威胁，故对外拒透其具体信息；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，终获释放；据悉，羁押期间，其曾被两次做强制性“精神病鉴定”。此前被羁押于上海市浦东新区看守所。张展自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日左右去到武汉报导当地疫情，一直在微信、推特、<span lang="EN-US">YouTube </span>等社交媒体平台上直播武汉的现场情况，并尽其所能地帮助受疫情影响的人维权。张展在武汉实地写了大量关于武汉疫情的真实报道。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在武汉遭“强迫失踪”，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被上海市浦东分局刑事拘留，被控罪名是寻衅滋事，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月遭正式逮捕。被起诉，其在狱中绝食抗议，身体状况极差。现羁押在浦东新区看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，张展女士案一审开庭，并当庭宣判，张展女士因言获罪被上海浦东新区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张珍华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川达州法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。四川省万源市茶品公司的退休职工。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日下午，张珍华正在友人毛坤家做客休息，又被成都市金牛区分局国保警察、茶店子派出所孟红等一伙警察疯狂砸门抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点半，被四川省成都市金牛区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张正廷：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省丹东市经济合作开发区访民、台属。张正廷于<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年投资于丹东市振兴区浪头镇的顺达微孔过滤器厂，到<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，张正廷投资的厂房恰好在丹东市城区公路扩建规划内而需要搬迁。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，地方政府在无任何手续的情况下，出动公安、城管以及社会人员几百号人，对张正廷的顺达过滤器厂层层包围，将厂房夷为平地。张正廷的妻子宋玉洁还被殴打致伤。正是在地方申诉无望的情况下，张正廷、宋玉洁夫妻才不得已进京告御状。想不到，这一告就是<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个年头，且每年的敏感时期都要被维稳，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年十八大前夕，丹东市政府提出给张正廷、宋玉洁夫妇俩<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元维稳补偿费，张正廷拒绝后被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。如此政府却诬陷其为敲诈勒索。张正廷今年已经<span lang="EN-US">76</span>岁，其在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日凌晨零点<span lang="EN-US">48</span>分，被辽宁省丹东市驻京维稳人员<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余人，闯入其位于北京市大兴区的暂住地，强行截回辽宁丹东。后被丹东市经济合作开发区公安分局刑拘，理由是张正廷涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被正式逮捕。羁押在丹东市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张志江：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赤峰市元宝山区五家镇小石头分金桥村居民，法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日晚在大水清道上被喀喇沁旗楼子店派出所警察绑架。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日上午，赤峰元宝山区五家镇村警李文明领着锦山公安局警察闯到张志江家非法抄家，在家里没人的情况下，搜走了大法书。并将张志江非法关押在喀喇沁旗锦山看守所。之后，喀喇沁旗公安局编造材料，将构陷张志江的案卷上报到喀喇沁旗检察院，检察院以张志江炼法轮功、悬挂真相条幅等理由，非法起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，内蒙古赤峰市喀喇沁旗法院开庭非法庭审法轮功学员张志江。张志江为自己做了无罪辩护。法院随后将张志江非法判刑，具体刑期不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">章军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省南充市蓬安县巨龙镇法法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年开始修炼法轮功，曾被中共抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被西城派出所警察抓捕、构陷；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被南充市顺庆区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵爱真</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：山东菏泽法轮功学员，女，生于<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年，菏泽市牡丹区糖果食品厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日傍晚，王翠英在路边发送真相册子时，被跟踪监控的牡丹区公安局警察抓捕。当日晚上，国保大队警察闯入独居的赵爱真家中，将她抓捕，并抄家，将家中的两台电脑、三台打印机、大法书、真相资料、光盘、打印纸等大量个人物品尽数抄走。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，王翠英、赵爱真两人被牡丹区公安分局刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，遭批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，鄄城县法院下的判决，王翠英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款两万元；赵爱真被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款一万五千元。赵爱真刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵帮海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川成都法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，成都市法轮功学员赵帮海、李常秋夫妇因宣传法轮功而被抓捕。后均遭枉判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑，那年他们的独生女儿十六岁。四年来，失去父母照顾的独生女儿多次要求会见冤狱中的父亲，却遭监狱无情的推诿、拒绝。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵晨宇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">昆明市女教师、法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十五岁，原是昆明市第三十中学一级教师，中文系研究生，是一位学生爱戴的好老师。赵晨宇曾于<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。赵晨宇于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初回西双版纳傣族自治州景洪市探望年迈的母亲，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日刚返回到昆明家中，就被跟踪而来的西双版纳景洪市国保大队警察抓捕、抄家。于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日在西双版纳再次被庭审，判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。被关押在西双版纳傣族自治州景洪市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵鄂川：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贵州省贵阳市法轮功学员。赵鄂川<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被警察绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点至<span lang="EN-US">11</span>点半遭贵阳市南明区法院被庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，南明区法院告知律师，对赵鄂川判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。赵鄂川提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，律师已经把赵鄂川的上诉状递交到贵阳市中级法院。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk54972182"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵根法：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk54972182;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵根法、黄春玲、刘洪兰、乔华荣四人都是山东省曲阜市的法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，黄春玲在刘洪兰家做客，赵根法、乔华荣夫妻去看她们，刚坐下还没说几句话，曲阜市国保大队人员就进入刘洪兰家，以「非法集会、集体学法」等罪名，将他们抓捕至书院派出所，另外以「把你的包拿过来看一下」为由将赵根法钥匙夺走，在赵根法、乔华荣夫妻二人都不在场、家中无人的情况下抄家，将法轮功书籍、手机、光盘、笔记本计算机、内存卡、</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk54972182;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">U</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk54972182;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">盘等几十件物品劫走。第二天，即<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，赵根法被关押在曲阜市拘留所；乔华荣、刘洪兰被送往济宁市看守所进行关押；黄春玲被关押在泗水县拘留所。后赵根法、黄春玲、刘洪兰、乔华荣，被抓捕、关押一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日遭济宁市任城区法院庭审，赵根法被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，黄春玲、刘洪兰被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，乔华荣被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。四人都被非法罚款一万元。赵根法刑期至：</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2023</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">赵国江</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：湖北省襄樊市人，襄樊铁路客运段职工，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信法轮功，早年曾被非法关押拘禁<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次，<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年被冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，赵国江被襄阳市樊城法院秘密非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，随后被送湖北省范家台监狱八监区服刑。出狱后，因他继续坚持信仰、宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日又被襄阳樊城区柿铺派出所警方刑拘，家被搜查，被关押在襄阳市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被襄阳市樊城法院再次以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。后被送往襄南监狱，但被拒收，又被送范家台监狱，因体检不合格拒收，现又关押在襄阳市第二看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">赵海军：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1966</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，黑龙江省哈尔滨市人，法轮功学员，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月因信仰法轮功，并与其妻等人为中共镇压、迫害法轮功到北京和平请愿，被当局抓捕，先被关押于哈尔滨双城市看守所，后又被送到双城区单城敬老院进行强制洗脑教育，期间因屡受虐待酷刑愤而绝食抗议，当局才不得不于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月将其释放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月因前往北京为法轮功进行和平请愿，而被北京警方抓捕，并被关押于北京市团河劳教所，直至一年多后方予以释放。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日因其屡次控告迫害法轮功的元凶江泽民，遂被当地警方从家中抓走，并被以涉邪教罪刑拘，其家遭查抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被双城区检察院转正式批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被哈尔滨双城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉，后虽经哈尔滨市中级法院二审，但依然维持原判。目前在黑龙江省呼兰监狱服刑。据悉，因在狱中遭遇虐待，致其长期不能排尿而被强制打针。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">赵海通：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1961</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日出生，青海省海西州人，新疆民主维权公民，中国在押政治犯。因长期致力于为新疆地区弱势群体、维吾尔族群体及政治犯、良心犯等维权呼吁，近年来又南下广东，积极与南方各地维权公民、人权捍卫者等一起参与街头民主运动，举行各种声援举牌和集会活动，故而在所处之地备受民众欢迎；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，曾因前往湖北武汉会见人权活动家秦永敏，惨遭武汉警方的野蛮殴打，差点丧命；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾因努力表达维权公民正当合法的诉求，而不惧风险在广州火车站多次举牌，宣传民主理念，“抗议流氓政府打压民主人士”等；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因参与声援安徽民主人士张林之女张安妮失学事件，而遭警方强行拘押；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，曾因在新疆吐鲁番市帮助维吾尔族公民进行维权，而被新疆警方刑拘，并被关押于新疆乌鲁木齐市六道湾看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被新疆警方宣布以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，终被新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐市法院以同罪名秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区塔城市乌苏市乌苏监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵怀国：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">基督徒，湖南省张家界市慈利县常驻居民，慈利县伯特利基督教会建立人，伯利恒教会主任牧师，中国在押良心犯。因笃信基督，而于，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年起从从东北到湖南省慈利县传福音，同年创办伯特利家庭教会，信徒多以年长者为主；因其所属教会曾多次被官方要求加入“三自教会”，均因价值理念不合而被其及教会众信徒拒绝，遂成为当局排挤、维稳打压的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾遭大批公安警方及宗教局人员闯入教会打砸；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，慈利县宗教局曾出动县民族宗教事务局、公安局、城管等部门近<span lang="EN-US">50</span>人，强行撬开伯特利教会大门，毁坏教会用品，撕毁墙上宗教信仰标志，并抄走《圣经》、诗歌本福音单张、钢琴等各类教会用品；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其被张家界市慈利县警方突然以涉嫌’煽动颠覆国家政权罪’刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被慈利县检察院以同罪名正式批捕，指控其因使用翻墙软件浏览境外媒体有关武汉疫情的报导，又转发嘲讽政府的打油诗等文字，属于严重危害国家安全行为；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其“煽动颠覆国家政权罪” 案在张家界市中级法院开庭受审，公诉方建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>个月，法官称将择日宣判。目前疑被羁押于慈利县看守所（湖南省张家界市慈利县零阳镇，邮政编号：<span lang="EN-US">427200</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，抚顺市新宾县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，赵杰和另一法轮功学员走在路上，被抚顺市新宾县公安局国保大队和派出所警察抓捕，在抚顺市第一看守所被关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被辽宁省抚顺市法轮功学员被抚顺市顺城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金两万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川西昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，被国安抓捕控制后抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><a name="_Hlk54973417"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵俊香：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk54973417;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省庆云县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，山东省庆云县公安局国保大队纠集几十个警察，抓捕了正在学习法轮大法著作的<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多名法轮功学员。根据长期电话监听和监控，警察又抓捕<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余人，共计<span lang="EN-US">46</span>人，其中大多数是<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁以上的老人，大部份法轮功学员被抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日上午，在庆云县法院，夏津县法院人员对六名仍被关押的庆云法轮功学员，赵俊香、王素娟、杜全村、段桂霞、于炳兰、张连云庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，山东夏津县法院开出判决书：赵俊香判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，杜全村判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，王素娟判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，于炳兰判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，张连云判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。赵俊香刑期至：</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2026</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵丽英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川内江法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，原在四川内江市铁路机务段小学教书，已退休，现居住内江铁路机械学校家属宿舍。在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，赵丽英在内江市区贴法轮功传单，被内江市中区公安分局派人跟踪，抓捕，并抄家，被关押到内江市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，赵丽英被构陷到了内江检察院。之后，家人、朋友一直没有得到任何信息。直到<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月底，赵丽英已经被非押一年多，家人去给她送衣物时，才被看守所人员告知，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，赵丽英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款二千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员，哈尔滨市轴承厂退休职工，现年已经七十岁了。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日上午，赵林在南岗区先锋路附近粘贴了一张“法轮大法好”不干胶，被南岗公安分局国保警察抓捕、抄家，抢走其家中法轮大法书籍。后获悉被判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵林（河北）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北张家口市桥东区法轮功学员。赵林<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日上午被张家口市公安局桥东分局<span lang="EN-US">51</span>路派出所警察抓捕，并抄走手机维修小店工作用的计算机，同时抄走法轮功资料。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，桥西区法院定对赵林开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月赵林被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵美华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邯郸法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，赵美华被复兴区刑警队和铁路大院派出所警察抓捕，被关押在邯郸第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下午，邯郸市磁县法院对赵美华视频开庭。后得知，赵美华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵明堂：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西省侯马市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月中旬赵明堂于被判刑四年。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵明堂是<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日左右在侯马市新田广场发真相资料时被警察绑架的，当天晚上被警察赵建林带人非法抄了家。第十天时，赵明堂被非法批捕。十一月中旬在曲沃法院被非法开庭时，赵明堂的儿子与弟弟进入了法庭。开庭中，赵明堂被戴手铐、脚镣，他大声喊“法轮大法好”。赵明堂曾在山西祁县监狱被非法关押七年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵仁霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生。山东省青岛法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日下午五点左右，赵仁霞从住处下楼，被青岛开发区公安分局国保大队警察绑架，而后把赵转移到户口管辖地灵珠山派出所。<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日下午五点左右，灵珠山派出所警察将赵押到青岛市普东看守所羁押。后遭批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，赵仁霞被青岛市黄岛区法院判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵任远：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广西桂林市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日半夜，谢建新与妻子赵任远被桂林市七星分局的派出所警察声称“测体温”闯入家中，搜查抄走<span lang="EN-US">1</span>轮功书籍、资料、法轮功币等物品，并抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被庭审，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日均被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵文静</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵文静、黄金桔、吕月霞、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连得。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵熙茹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员：石香云、贾艳玲、包义、魏续旺、孔庆艳、朱凤英、赵熙茹、刘君、任秀英、杨骐骥、吴樨、张树霞、宫文义。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被松北区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵兴有：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江法轮功学员赵兴有，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">79</span>岁，和老伴史桂芝，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十七岁，家住黑龙江省哈尔滨市双城区水泉乡。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，双城房产一工作人员去赵兴有夫妇所居住的水泉乡赵家村一村民家，给该村民的房屋拍照，发现赵兴有夫妇家的院墙上喷写有“法轮大法好”的字样，此工作人员心生恶念，把字样拍照下来，传给双城区公安局、六一零。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，警察将赵兴有夫妇抓捕。送哈尔滨做身体检查后，因史桂芝身体不合格，被放回家，赵兴有被劫持到双城看守所，关押六天放回。放回后，指使保人监视他们，不准往墙上写字、不准去炼功点、不准接触修炼人等。后双城公安局警察将赵兴有、史桂芝夫妇构陷到哈尔滨市法院，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，法院法逮捕通知书，水泉乡派出所苏永生等又将赵兴有、史桂芝夫妇再次绑架，赵兴有被劫持到双城看守所非法关押，史桂芝因检查身体不合格放回。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，史桂芝再次被非法抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月上旬，赵兴有被冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，史桂芝被冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。史桂芝被劫持到黑龙江省女子监狱，赵兴有被劫入哈尔滨市呼兰监狱。赵兴有刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵秀娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">武汉市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，刘社红和妻子赵秀娟在荆州市被抓捕，被关押在荆州市荆州区西门看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日获悉，刘社红被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，妻子赵秀娟被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵颜华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年生，系北京首安消防公司工程师。赵颜华于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日上午，被李桥派出所警察抓捕，当晚送往顺义看守所。关押十个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被北京市顺义区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚金三千元。判决书声称：“本院依法组成合议庭，公开开庭审理了本案。”却不让家人亲属参与旁听。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郑旭飞</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：男，<span lang="EN-US">42</span>岁，山东省乳山市下初镇中心学校体育教师，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，郑旭飞曾因宣传法轮功信息而被警方抓捕，在抓捕过程中，因野蛮抓捕，当被警察拖上警车时，他的锁骨已被摔成骨折，之后被送往看守所刑拘。被关押期间，被戴着手铐脚镣<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个多月，并遭毒打和被逼做奴工。<span lang="EN-US">35</span>天后被强迫交<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元钱准予取保候审。因他被无理关押迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年的绩效工资两万元被他所在单位扣除。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，郑旭飞又因宣传法轮功资料而被乳山市警方抓捕，后被乳山市检察院正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被乳山市法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，山东省威海中级法院二审维持非法，并追加罚款罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郑艳梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北辛集法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，河北省辛集市南智邱镇南棚村李月棉和辛集市马庄乡北营村郑艳梅、边彦娟因讲法轮功真相被大屯派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日第二次开庭，律师又充分的做了无罪辩护，法官说结果要等通知，然后因为疫情一直到三月份律师才得知结果，三人都被判刑，刑期分别为：李月棉<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元；郑艳梅<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">9</span>千元；边彦娟<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年三个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。后得知，这三名法轮功学员已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日都被关押到石家庄女子监狱服刑。郑艳梅刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">钟国权：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年生，身体极度。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日上午，钟国权在黑龙江密山县大街上发真相资料被密山市利民派出所（二所）警察抓捕，后刑事拘留，因身体有病，被取保候审。钟国权于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被密山法院开庭审理，第二天，钟国权被强行送进鸡西看守所。几天后，钟国权家人接到法院非法判决钟国权<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的判决书。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">钟华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">成都青年法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，钟华、冉文芳在街上给一个人讲了大法真相，当她们离开后，这个人拨打<span lang="EN-US">110</span>恶意举报，驷马桥派出所通过监控，找到正在回家路上的钟华和冉文芳，将她们抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，钟华和冉文芳被成都金牛区法院判刑，钟华<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万，冉文芳<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金六千元。她们上诉后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，成都市中院法院对她们维持原判。钟华和冉文芳被非法关押在成都郫县看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">钟兴秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">江西省武宁县人，法轮功学员，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年期间，曾因组织、参与制作、印刷法轮功宣传光盘、书刊等行动，传授打印、刻录、装订技术等，而遭到地方当局严密监控和打击。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在与他人搬运、携带<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年神韵晚会光盘、《明慧周刊》等相关海外法轮功影像杂志资料时，被武宁县警方获悉，当场拘捕，其家被抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其被江西省武宁县人民法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，经九江市中级人民法院二审依然驳回起诉，维持原判。目前被羁押于江西省武宁县看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">钟义芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，攀枝花市攀钢集团公司第二机械厂退休工人，法轮功学员。自从中共开始迫害法轮功后，钟义芳非法劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年钟义芳被判刑八年，于<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被关押到四川省龙泉驿女子监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月才出狱回家<span lang="EN-US">.2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月又遭中共当局抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月获悉，钟义芳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。她现在被迫害得出现严重的尿毒症，骨瘦如柴，肚子肿的老大，每天看守所给她打针。生命健康令人担忧。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">仲周（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年出生，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州人，又叫“尊珠”，阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因其协助侄子兼徒弟、同寺僧人彭措（又叫平措，已于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日自焚死亡，时年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>岁）为纪念中共当局镇压拉萨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>•<span lang="EN-US">14</span>事件三周年，抗议中共政府对藏人的强权高压统治，以自焚方式（指一种藏人抗议暴政、伸张正义的方式，即藏人自焚者把自己整个奉献出来，以清晰的理智、自愿的心态和惨烈的方式向暴政表达最强烈抗议的无奈选择，以期使公众舆论对极权和高压统治者予以最强烈的谴责或改变对手的情感）在阿坝县城洽唐中街实施自焚行动；同时，因其担心当局野蛮抢夺自焚尸体，而将自焚后的彭措转移隐藏到格尔登寺内，由此引发中共军警与当地僧人、藏人的激烈对抗和冲突；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，其随被阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康县警方抓捕，并被以“安排转移、藏匿彭措达<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个小时之久，导致彭措因为体表大面积烧伤、延误救治而死亡”为罪由刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被四川省马尔康县法院以“故意杀人罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周嫦兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月出生，家住广州市白云区。周嫦兰（周常兰）因正义销毁白云区景泰北社区多次出现的诽谤、诬陷法轮功的邪恶宣传栏，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，在白云区景泰街云苑南禁毒广场，被白云区公安分局和白云区景泰派出所警察抓捕，被关押到白云区看守所。直到<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，才得知周嫦兰被秘密关押、判刑的消息。周嫦兰被荔湾区检察院起诉，遭荔湾区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周翠萍<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省连云港市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，连云港市海州区公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘玉萍、邵世玲、那仁志、熊成霞、周翠萍、马宝玲、高建君、王艾芝、汪宝玉、小周女士、乔老太等十一人。所有人家中都被非法抄了家，警察劫走家中的电脑、手机、光盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘、电器、钱财、书籍等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，周翠萍被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周德元</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：长沙市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁，家住在长沙市左家塘附近的烟草公司宿舍。从一九九八年，周德元开始修炼法轮功。她是一位开朗的常德人，用湖南人都能听懂的常德话和人们交流。从常德市轴承厂退休后，她与家人迁居到了长沙。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，周德元被抓捕，十五天行政拘留结束，又被关押在长沙市第四看守所。后，周德元被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被转送至湖南省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周殿文</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：黑龙江省哈尔滨市依兰县法轮功学员。男，七十多岁，原中煤黑龙江省依兰县达连河煤矿退休工人，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月份发法轮功台历时，被人诬告，被依兰县公安局国保大队队长杨维兴带人抓捕到看守所。周殿文老人，被关押一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年末被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，目前在黑龙江省泰来监狱遭受关押迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周海燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大连公安局国保支队同大连开发区公安分局属下五彩城派出所、湾里派出所、黄海路派出所、海青派出所、董家沟派出所等出动数十个警察，以拦路抓捕、抢劫、入室抢劫的方式在多个地点同时实施多起抓捕法轮功学员案。十名当时被抓捕的法轮功学员被非法批捕：周海燕、胡志琴（女，五十八岁）、来桂芳（女，四十二岁）、时宁瑶（女，三十八岁）、方芳（女，五十四岁）、林景萍（女，四十六岁）、贾秀春（女，四十一岁）、曹娥（女，五十五岁）、武丽艳（女，五十二岁）和刘淑芬（女，七十八岁）。八十一岁的郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被取保候审。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月八名法轮功学员被大连开发区法院判刑：周海燕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，胡志琴<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，来桂芳<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，时宁瑶<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，林景萍<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，方芳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，贾秀春<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。周海燕刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周金莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南省郴州市永兴县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十一岁的周金莲是永兴县的一个普通家庭妇女，家住湖南省郴州市永兴县沙子光。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，周金莲在永兴县鲤鱼塘镇向民众讲述法轮功真相，被鲤鱼塘派出所的警察抓捕，之后被关押在郴州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月下旬，周金莲被永兴县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周模珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川古蔺县古蔺镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，法轮功学员周模珍和骆雪梅在习水县醒民镇钢铁村，告诉百姓法轮功真相，被举报。醒民镇派出所抓捕了周模珍和骆雪梅<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，周模珍和骆雪梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周娜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西太原市万柏林区法轮功学员。周绍山、高继萍夫妻与女儿周娜<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被警察绑架、抄家，在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月左右，周绍山被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元，高继萍被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元，周娜被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周启良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">周启良、王传煌、汪黎明三人均系江西省武宁县人，法轮功学员，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年期间，曾因组织、参与制作、印刷法轮功宣传光盘、书刊等行动，学习、传授打印、刻录、装订等技术，使用具有自动拨号及语音功能的手机给他人打电话等，而遭到地方当局严密监控和打击。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在共同搬运、携带<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年神韵晚会光盘、《明慧周刊》等相关海外法轮功影像杂志资料时，被武宁县警方获悉，当场拘捕，其家分别被抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人均被江西省武宁县人民法院一审以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。其三人均表不服，提起上诉，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，经九江市中级人民法院二审依然驳回起诉，维持原判。目前都被羁押于江西省武宁县看守所。分别刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生。一人独居在贵阳云岩区省政府大院，她父亲是贵州省政府一名老干部。周琴毕业于贵州大学外语学院，后在贵州省教育学院任教，是一名大学英语教师；由于大学期间的一次事故，摔断脚踝造成残疾。周琴<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年以前就修炼法轮功。周琴<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月遭当局抓捕，家人不知。后表姐和友人们多方查询，在离贵阳市很远的“贵阳市三江女子看守所”查到周琴被关押里面。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日周琴被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，周琴的家人近期收到法院判决书。据说周琴被关押在贵阳羊艾第一女子监狱。因为疫情，家人还没有见到周琴。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周绍山：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西太原市万柏林区法轮功学员。周绍山、高继萍夫妻与女儿周娜<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被警察绑架、抄家，在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月左右，周绍山被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元，高继萍被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元，周娜被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">周世峰：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，河南省安阳县人，北京锋锐律师事务所主任，<span lang="EN-US"> 2009</span>年度、<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年度“社会公益法律服务先进个人”、<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年中国法律援助“优秀援助律师”、<span lang="EN-US"> 2009-2011</span>年度“北京优秀律师”，知名人权律师。自<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年执业以来，曾代理过多起著名的受害人案件，并于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月创立北京锋锐律师事务所，广纳包括王宇、刘晓原、王全章等在内的著名人权律师。<span lang="EN-US"> 2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被北京市警方以“严重扰乱社会秩序”、“教唆、组织、策划、资助他人炒作所谓敏感案件” 等为罪由抓走刑拘，其锋锐律师事务所及其办公室被查抄。被指定居所监视居住，其锋锐律师事务所及其办公室被查抄；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被天津市警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被天津市第二中级法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。现羁押在天津市第一看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周维林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安徽合肥人权捍卫者、工伤致残人士。周维林<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，原安徽省拖拉机厂退休职工，维权网信息员，安徽省维权人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年曹顺利人权捍卫者奖获得者。曾于<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日因工受伤，成为丧失劳动能力的伤残人员，但原所在单位一直不给于办理伤残认定和退休等手续，自此走上维权之路。自<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年起，尤其是<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年期间，因长期坚持实名报导安徽及全国各地多种公权力违法侵权事件，并成为“维权网”信息员，而招致当局的强烈不满和忌恨，曾先后<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次被合肥警方处以行政拘留，并且多次被警方抄家、传唤、威胁甚至殴打。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，各地维权人士发起声援“安妮失学事件”的活动，周维林因前往进行实时报导，而被合肥警方于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日强行带走，处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，又因参与合肥网友聚餐纪念<span lang="EN-US">64</span>活动，遭到警方的报复性拘留，之后获释；但时至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，合肥警方再次因<span lang="EN-US">64</span>纪念活动而以“涉嫌虚构事实扰乱公共秩序”事由对其进行传唤，并处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，合肥警方第三次以参与声援安妮失学事件，维护安妮受教育权活动为由，将其与张林、李化平、姚诚等维权人士一同拘捕，并以涉嫌“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”而刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被当地检察院以同罪名正式批捕，之后被安徽省合肥市地方法院以“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，刑满获释。出狱后仍然在一直坚持为劳工和残疾人维权。周维林于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被合肥市公安局瑶海分局城东派出所（电话：<span lang="EN-US">0551-64483496</span>）秘密抓走了。后获悉遭刑事拘留、逮捕。周维林案已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日在合肥开庭审理，未当庭宣判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周喜云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郑州市法轮功学员。女，四十多岁。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，周喜云在荆建秋家中做客，她俩一起被荥阳广武派出所警察、荥阳国保大队警察抓捕，被关押在郑州第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，在中原区法院南办公区被开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月下旬，荆建秋和周喜云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚款三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周显蓉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川西昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，被国安抓捕控制后抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，勒索处罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span
