lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周向阳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津法轮功学员。周向阳从北方交通大学毕业后，分配到天津铁道第三勘探设计院工经处，因工作出色，单位送他到天津大学，又获得投资经济学位；<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>考取了全国首批造价工程师职业资格，成为当时全国仅有的六十位造价工程师之一。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，期间遭受无数酷刑：被彻夜电击至遍体鳞伤、连续三十天熬夜、多次关小号、野蛮灌食等等。周向阳在<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被绑架后，于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，后到天津市滨海监狱原五监区二分监区（现六监区）服刑，一直绝食抵制迫害。一开始，狱警安排六个包夹人（监狱安排的专门负责看管法轮功学员的刑事罪犯人）白天晚上轮流看管周向阳，每天包夹人用担架抬着周向阳去监狱的医院灌食三次。据包夹人说：“有一次给周向阳灌食，包夹人按着他的胳膊和双腿，监狱医院的人强行把胃管从周向阳的嘴里插进去，灌完食之后，周向阳自己把胃管拔出来，管子上面沾满了鲜血。”妻子李珊珊因坚持为丈夫申冤，曾遭到监狱的报复，两次被非法劳教共计三年多。二零一三年劳教制度解体了，李珊珊是从石家庄女子劳教所走出来的最后一个。一家人团聚的日子没有多久。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日早晨七点，天津警察再一次破门而入，把周向阳和妻子李珊珊抓走了。周向阳被冤判七年，李珊珊被冤判六年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周兴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市金州区石河镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚，谷秀华（女）、刘希永（男）、周兴（男）、李天学（男）、王丽志（女）、张三曼（女）、谭春荣（女）、孙宝英（女）、刘井龙（男），去大连市金普新区炮台镇袁屯村发放新书《共产主义的终极目的》，被炮台镇派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午二在大连市金州法院庭审。后谷秀华、周兴、王丽志，被大连市金州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；张三曼、谭春荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，李天学被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刘希永、孙宝英、刘井龙的情况还不清楚。周兴刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周妍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">46</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。周研被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年， 处罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周艳波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市金州区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，周艳波毕业于大连医科大学附属卫校，由国家统一分配到大连开发区医院工作，从事临床护理工作。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年，周艳波开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，没有经过任何法律程序，周艳波被劫持到了马三家劳教所，被劳教两年。遭酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被国保警察抓捕后，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被视频非法开庭，周艳波被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。目前，周艳波仍被非法关押在大连姚家看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周永杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省农安县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生，家住长春市农安县，常在长春市打工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，周永杰被长春市朝阳区宽平派出所抓捕。关押在长春市第四看守所。此后家属未得到任何信息。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年底，周永杰被关押在长春市女子监狱后，家属才得知，她被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周永林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁锦州凌海市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，孙继萍与丈夫周永林被中共绑架、关押，劳教，在派出所、看守所、劳教所遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，孙继萍与丈夫周永林在盘锦市锦采新区大集上告诉人们“法轮大法好”时，被凌海市公安局闫家镇派出所警察绑架，被隔离二十一天后（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日），孙继萍被非法关押到锦州市女子看守所，周永林被非法关押到凌海市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，凌海市法院对孙继萍与丈夫周永林每人各判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、罚金各一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周玉香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东平度市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>岁生，是平度大泽山镇尹家村一位普通的农村妇女。周玉香<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日与外甥女周君、好友展中香一起到平度仁兆赶集，被仁兆派出所警察抓捕并被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午，周玉香被青岛市黄岛区法院在即墨市普东看守所，通过视频非法庭审，律师做了有理有据的无罪辩护，最后，周玉香被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周远志：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周远志（笔名华梁兴、曾仁全）<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日生。是一名自由撰稿人、独立中文笔会会员，由于长期撰写、发表关于各类社会问题及揭露官员腐败的文章，在<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被湖北省钟祥市国家安全局以“涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪”抓捕，获释后周远志在家长期被当局监视居住。根据独立中文笔会的网页显示，他以笔名曾仁全发表多篇敏感文章，其中题目包括“农民以特殊方式表达对江泽民的憎恶”及“人民的名义远离普世价值”。周远志被<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被以“织非法聚集罪”刑事拘留。此前，周远志被指组织访民上访而被当局关押，，被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天原本应于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日释放，但未获释放，随后，被确认其在<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日即遭湖北荆门市公安局东宝分局以“织非法聚集罪”刑事拘留。其妻子张中凤说由于他一向身体不好，她非常担心丈夫的情况。现羁押在荆门市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日在荆门掇刀法院开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日以“组织非法聚集罪判刑期<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，网上寻衅滋事罪<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，诽谤罪<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，决定合并执行<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月”，刑期<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。目前关押地址：<a name="_Hlk52057464">湖北省荆门市东宝区牌楼镇荆门看守所，电话<span lang="EN-US">0724-8882273</span>，邮编<span lang="EN-US">448121<o:p></o:p></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52057464;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">周育琴</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52057464;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：广东省惠东县人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信仰、宣传法轮功，周育琴与石雪梅、刘庆强三人，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被惠东县政法委、<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办及国保等警方非法抓捕，后于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被广东省惠州市惠东县法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密宣判。其中，周育琴被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并处罚金五万元<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日</b>）；石雪梅被冤判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）；刘庆强被冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）。三人均不服审判，已向广东省惠州市中级法院提出上诉。</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">目前被关押在惠东县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周再强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南长沙网民。职业货车司机。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月网上发言支持香港反送中的光复香港、时代革命运动被刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，周再强的亲友才在微信发出消息称：长沙公民周再强近期因在推特上发言支持香港反送中运动而被当局突然抓捕，并以寻衅滋事的罪名刑事拘留，目前已经确认被关押于长沙市第一看守所。据了解，周再强有两个匿名推特号，已持续发推三万多条。香港反送中运动爆发后，他一直都非常关注，也自发和转发了很多推文表示关注和支持。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱承志：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">人权捍卫者。朱承志早年与友人合资在云南经营锰矿场，其后被新加入的拍档施计夺去矿场，而对方更抢先入禀法院状告朱承志侵吞矿场。结果，朱承志被判败诉，多年资产化为乌有。他多次向公安厅投诉均不获受理，只好进京上访，却遭关押<span lang="EN-US">40</span>天。朱承志遂在网上组织民间维权运动，包括声援“福州三网友”案。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，他又冒险到医院探望近乎失聪失明的同乡兼同窗“六四铁汉”李旺阳，并协助香港媒体为李作生前唯一一次专访。由于他拒绝在“不再关注李旺阳死亡事件保证书”上签字，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被湖南省公安厅以“扰乱社会治安”之名拘留；其家人于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日收到朱承志的逮捕通知书，指朱承志被省公安控以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”。后获释。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月与谭作人、艾晓明共同荣获中国民主教育基金会颁发的<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年度杰出民主人士奖。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日因祭奠林昭后已遭强迫失踪，后获知其被控“寻衅滋事”而被指定居所监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，林昭祭日当天，朱承志另外<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名维权人士，成功到达苏州灵岩山林昭墓前祭奠。随后，大批警察当场把<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人带走，当中<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人后来获释，但朱承志却和外界失去联系。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日上午，苏州市吴中区法院以寻衅滋事罪名宣判著名人权捍卫者朱承志朱承志<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱凤英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员：石香云、贾艳玲、包义、魏续旺、孔庆艳、朱凤英、赵熙茹、刘君、任秀英、杨骐骥、吴樨、张树霞、宫文义。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被松北区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">朱桂贞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">山东泰安市法轮功信徒，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁的老太太，原泰安市木器厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日下午，朱桂贞和平秀英为了让民众了解法轮大法，在邱家店镇某村，发送法轮功资料，并向路人讲述法轮功受迫害的真相，遭邱家店派出所警察绑架，被关到泰安市看守所。后于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，朱桂贞因修炼法轮功，向百姓传播法轮大法，被泰安市泰山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱海燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宁夏银川市永宁县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年生。大学本科毕业，原宁夏银川市永宁县环境监测中心工作人员，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年底开始修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，朱海燕多次被抓捕、被关押、劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，朱海燕等<span lang="EN-US">14</span>名法轮功学员被银川市永宁县公安局恶警抓捕、抄家，朱海燕被关押在银川市看守所，后被银川市永宁县公安局构陷到银川市西夏区检察院；遭银川市永宁县公安局和银川市西夏区检察院相互勾结迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被银川市西夏区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">朱惠来：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">广东省湛江市人，广东省湛江市东海岛东山镇调青北园村村民，抗强拆维权者，民间誉名“东海岛英雄”，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年以来，广东省湛江市政府以“湛江钢铁基地”为名，在无任何批文的前提下（注：该批文直至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日才拿到，总值人民币<span lang="EN-US">700</span>亿），烂用公权，派出大批警力对该区域东海岛东简镇衔头村、迈奴村、蓄昌村等八条村以及东山镇北园村等一万多名村民进行暴力拆迁，致使万民怨声载道；因之前朱惠来父子一家不愿意为强拆签字，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，湛江市开发区官员随带领数十人，在没有支付拆迁款的情况下，强毁其田地和家园里的果树、帐棚和农作物等；其子朱培忍开车回来，看到父亲被警方殴打，随前往和其一起与警方、强拆官员发生激烈对抗，最终导致<span lang="EN-US">1</span>死多伤（其中致当地治安大队副队长死亡）；随后，其立即被警方刑拘和逮捕，但却被民间誉为“东海岛英雄”。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被广东省湛江市赤坎区中级法院以“故意杀人罪”、“故意伤害罪”一审判处死刑；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，经湛江市赤坎区中级法院二审，改判死缓；其不服，继续上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，广东省高级法院对其案以“事实不清、证据不足”为由“撤销原判、发还重审”；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东省湛江市中级法院再次重审朱惠来父子抗强拆杀官员案，仍判死刑。　<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，广东高院（<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>）粤刑终<span lang="EN-US">298</span>号判决书作出终审判决：朱惠来犯故意杀人罪、故意伤害罪，决定执行死刑，缓期二年执行，剥夺政治权利终身，并限制减刑。目前被羁押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱家彩：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贵州毕节威宁县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十多岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因发放法轮功资料挂横幅，朱家彩、罗翠琴遭抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在毕节七星关区法院被庭审，后得知朱家彩被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款二万元、罗翠琴被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，勒索罚款一万元。朱家彩刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">朱培忍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：广东省湛江市人，广东湛江东海岛东山镇调青北园村村民，“东海岛英雄”，抗暴维权者。自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年以来，广东省湛江市政府以“湛江钢铁基地”为名，在无任何批文的前提下（注：该批文直至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日才拿到，总值人民币<span lang="EN-US">700</span>亿），烂用公权，派出大批警力对该区域东海岛东简镇衔头村、迈奴村、蓄昌村等八条村以及东山镇北园村等一万多名村民进行暴力拆迁，致使万民怨声载道；因之前朱培忍和其父一家不愿意为强拆签字，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，湛江市开发区官员随带领数十人，在没有支付拆迁款的情况下，强毁其父田地和家园里的果树、帐棚和农作物等，其父被严重殴打；其开车回来，看到父亲被警方殴打，随上前与父亲一起与警方、强拆官员发生激烈对抗，最终导致<span lang="EN-US">1</span>死多伤，其随被警方拘捕，但被民间誉为“东海岛英雄”。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被广东省湛江市赤坎区中级法院以“故意杀人罪”、“故意伤害罪”一审判处死缓。其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月经湛江市赤坎区中级法院二审，改判为无期徒刑。其依然不服，继续上诉，至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，广东省高级法院对其案以“事实不清、证据不足”为由“撤销原判、发还重审”。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日湛江市中级法院再审朱惠来父子抗暴杀官案，仍为无期徒刑。目前被关押地点不详。其在看守所惨遭酷刑，肝部被打裂，生殖器被打烂，牙齿被打掉，为此曾被送医院抢救。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱素荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，家住河北保定蠡县鲍墟乡东孟尝村，在中孟尝小学任教。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，正在学校上课的朱素荣，突然被鲍墟乡派出所警察骚扰，他们并尾随至家中抄家捕人，当天朱素荣就被送至保定看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月二<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被高阳法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月、勒索罚金五万元，朱素荣已上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱宇飙：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月出生，广东省人，原广州地铁小额贷款有限公司职员，原广东金粤律师事务所、广州市广大律师事务所、广东恒益律师事务所执业律师，广东省第一个公开为法轮功信仰者作无罪辩护的正义律师，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。学生时代，曾就读于广东省中山大学法学专业；法学硕士毕业后，先后曾就职于广东金粤律师事务所、广州市广大律师事务所和广东恒益律师事务所，作执业律师；因为经常热心为弱势群体当事人作代理辩护律师，并以低价或折价收费，甚至不计报酬，所以深受社会大众及业界同仁称许、好评；但因其练习和信仰法轮功而屡遭政府打压逼迫，遂被迫多次转换律所，直至最终其律师执业证被广东司法当局吊销；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年，曾分别为三名法轮功信仰者做无罪辩护，因其法庭辩护词精彩绝伦，堪称经典，顿令中共法庭大为震惊和难堪，随后即被广东司法当局称为“反革命”，将其列为广东省公安厅要维稳严控的“头号人物”；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其突然被广州市警方野蛮抓捕，后被枉法处劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，送广州市第三劳教所关押；关押期间，曾遭多次酷刑折磨，如“坐老虎凳”、“架飞机”、用湿毛巾盖脸窒息、水淹、在冷天灌凉水、鞭打手指及脚趾、不准睡觉，等等；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，劳教释放后，因其律师证被广州当局故意拖延办理，对其工作和日常生活造成极大不便；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其第二次被广州市海珠区新港派出所警方莫名抓捕、刑拘，家遭查抄，后被广州市海珠区法院以“利用邪教破坏法律实施罪”枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并送广东省北江监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，虽是其刑满获释日，但又被转送到广东省三水洗脑班非法关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，再次被广州市海珠区警方十余人闯入抄家，搜走几本其个人阅读的法轮功书籍之后，随即将其绑架到一不知名的法轮功洗脑班关押；据悉，自其被抓至今，家人一直无法知其更多信息。目前被羁押地点不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱兆水：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省舒兰市吉舒镇法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。一九九八年开始修炼法轮功。曾被非法劳教一年多。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日晚被当地警方抓捕、关押；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月中旬获悉，朱兆水被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">祝亚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武汉市黄陂区法轮功学员，祝亚是个残疾人，家住武汉市黄陂区前川街，丈夫早逝，她与女儿相依为命。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，祝亚去买菜，被便衣警察拦截。这次抓捕祝亚是由省城“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”亲自操控、指使的，他们闯进家中抄家。武汉市黄陂区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日庭审，被秘密枉判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">珠扎（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">现年<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县求吉玛乡索日玛村人，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。因政治诉求，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年曾被当局以不详政治罪名抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被警方以涉嫌“组织阿坝民众举办达赖喇嘛<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁寿辰活动”为罪由，从其僧舍强行带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其已被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 119.25pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">珠玛别克<span lang="EN-US">.</span>穆汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">42</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，新疆阿尔泰市人，阿尔泰市喀拉希力克乡武装部官员，哈萨克族政治犯。曾因被新疆中共当局指控在聊天工具微信“乱说话”，“泄漏中共党内机密”，而于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被阿尔泰市警方刑拘、逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，获悉近期已被新疆阿尔泰市法院以“泄露国家机密罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。据称，其原本在上海读大学的儿子因父亲被判刑，竟遭株连，被校方勒令退学，现已回到新疆家中。其妻子古丽加丽拉也因受牵连，原本在乡政府卫生院工作，也因此被辞退，他本人在银行的<span lang="EN-US">60</span>万元人民币积蓄遭罚没，家里的<span lang="EN-US">50</span>头牛也被政府没收。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">庄友布：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">42</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，福建省宁德市福鼎县人，法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，与肖传雄、金丽燕、陈星光、杨贵媚、杨雄、陈开奇，林丽芳、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄，至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，庄友布被宁德市检察院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，庄友布被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邹华兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，今年<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生，重庆长寿区法轮功学员，原重庆长寿农机公司退休职工，邹华兰因修炼法轮功曾多次遭受迫害：<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次劳教，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次判刑，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被关洗脑班，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次关押在看守所将近<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，中共政法委书记郭声琨到重庆开会，要求对跨区域活动的维权人士、法轮功学员等要重点打击。重庆市长寿区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>和国保为了完成所谓的“政治任务”，也为了捞取升官资本，开始寻找他们的下手目标。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，邹华兰在贵州结束冤狱回家。因为这段被外省判刑的经历，邹华兰成了长寿区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>和国保的迫害对象。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日左右，长寿区国保支队指使晏家街道派出所警察，到贵州去调查邹华兰被构陷的案子，作为再次迫害的“证据”。然后，又以监控摄像头摄到邹华兰在晏家街道发台历为借口，晏家派出所几个警察，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">33</span>日，闯入邹华兰家中，把邹华兰抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，邹华兰被逮捕，后被关押在长寿区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，邹华兰被重庆市江北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邹佩霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东东营法轮功学员。耿录堂、邹佩霞老夫妻，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年已年过七旬，家住东营市胜利油田孤岛采油厂芙蓉小区。修炼大法前，夫妻俩身体很不好，耿录堂还患有高血压等疾病。一九九六年前后，老俩口修炼法轮大法。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，老俩口去河口地区赶集，向人宣传法轮功，遭人恶告，东营市河口区国保大队下属的义和镇派出所警察，于当天抓捕了夫妇俩。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月开庭，后耿录堂、邹佩霞夫妇均被东营市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并被勒索罚款三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">左洪涛</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：秦皇岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦皇岛市山海关公安分局在左洪涛、崔秋荣夫妇开的“佳合中介”抓捕了夫妻二人及吴文章、杨晓勇、袁素静及李国爱等五名法轮功学员，抄查中野蛮地抢劫了中介周转资金十余万元现金及电动车一辆和其它办公用品。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，山海关区检察院侦监科科长陈铁忠对左洪涛、崔秋荣等人以莫须有的罪名非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，昌黎县法院对四名法轮功学员左洪涛、刘长富、吴文章、李国爱与左洪涛的妻子崔秋荣（不炼功）五人开庭。后判处左洪涛<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，吴文章<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，李国爱<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刘长富<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，左洪涛妻子崔秋荣（没炼功）<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零几个月（已获释）。左洪涛刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">结束语：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑满释放：<span lang="EN-US">26</span>人<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈淑梅、陈贤忠、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">戴学林、高连红、高文淑、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杭霞、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span>何华、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span>侯巧珍、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">蒋立宇、鞠小林、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李瑞华、李天学、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">李媛、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘美廷、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">马月琴、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">牛占华、冉文芳、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">单珊、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王文卿、吴锐、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">扎西加、战玉彩、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">赵春侠、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵广军、赵桂春、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱纯荣、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">迫害致死：<span lang="EN-US">1</span>人<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">毛坤<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、陈淑梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省白山市靖宇县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生在山东，在中共人为制造的大饥荒年代，小小年纪随父母逃荒到东北。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，陈淑梅在靖宇县江边，靖宇县公安局国保大队大队长于学军等七八个人绑架，野蛮地将陈淑梅拖到家中，完全没有顾及陈淑梅双侧股骨头坏死的剧烈疼痛，在未出示警察证、没有搜查证、没有立案决定书的情况下，强行抄家，抢走陈淑梅的大量大法书籍、师父法像和手机、笔记本电脑等私人物品。后行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，陈淑梅被刑事拘留，被送到白山市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，陈淑梅被吉林省白山市靖宇县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、陈贤忠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贵阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁高龄时被中共贵阳市南明区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，贵阳市南明区二十多名警察，在陈贤忠家里抓捕了包括陈贤忠夫妇在内的九名法轮功学员；陈贤忠家当日被抄家后，夫妇俩被抓捕到花果园派出所，第二天被送往贵阳市烂泥沟洗脑班非法关押<span lang="EN-US">12</span>天。回家后花果园派出所要求陈贤忠夫妇在半年内每天按时去派出所报到，过程中陈夫妇不断指出这是违法行为后，又改为每周一报到一次。一周后，陈夫妇再次拒绝报到。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，警察上门再次将陈夫妇抓捕到花果园派出所。陈贤忠被单独审讯六、七个小时后，被转移到贵阳市南明区看守所，他的夫人回家。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日前后，陈贤忠家人接到南明区法院下的判决通知书，陈贤忠被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">3</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、戴学林</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代中期出生，籍贯不详，广西师范大学出版社《理想国》品牌营销编辑，广西师范大学出版社北京贝贝特公司营销部重要负责人，人称广西师大理想国的主页君，知名网络推手，公益活动推动者。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年始，曾因利用微博做了一项“死活读不下去作品”的调查统计，从而引起网络热议，使之意识到自己可发挥更大作用，围绕“读书”做一些吸引年轻人关注力，以及既有趣又有意的公益活动；自<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年起，因与他人合作在中国大陆转售多种被中共当局视为政治禁书（例如高华的著作《红太阳是怎样升起的》等）的港台书籍，随引起中共当局警觉与监视；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，因与合作人张晓雄以合作营销、四六分成方式，由其负责用微信号“禁忌的游戏”（<span lang="EN-US">jinjideyouxi2014</span>）出售多项港台书籍，并由张晓雄负责入书和寄给买家，合伙销售<span lang="EN-US">1300</span>余本，后被中共当局知晓，即将销售款中的部分金额作为被抓判刑时的罪由加以指控；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，因从深圳网上书店“壹仁网”负责人杨海玲处购买港台书籍共计￥<span lang="EN-US">17</span>万余元，利用微信号“禁忌的游戏”推广，并由杨海玲直接寄给购书者，后被中共当局获悉，随将其销售额中的￥<span lang="EN-US">9</span>万余元视为“非法出版物”涉案金额；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其被警方突然从北京工作地点抓走，自此失联，直至同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月家属才知其被抓确切消息；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，警方又在其合作人张晓雄南京的住处及车库中搜走拟出售的其余图书<span lang="EN-US">291</span>本书，其中<span lang="EN-US">288</span>本后来亦被警方以“非法出版物”作为指控罪由；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年初其案件被当局开庭受理，至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日获悉，其已在近日被中共法院以“非法经营罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。目前被羁押地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、高连红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省高密市拒城河社区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日高连红被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">5</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、高文淑：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，山东省青岛市城阳区流亭赵村人，法轮功学员。因信仰法轮功而被青岛市当局多次绑架迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日下午，高文淑和丈夫邵承洛在夏庄镇发法轮功宣传材料时，被当地治安人员告发，当场即被夏庄派出所警方以涉“邪教罪”抓走，其家被查抄四次，并且警方在没有出具任何凭据的情况下，劫走家里二万元现金及许多物品。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，城阳区法院在城阳看守所内设法庭，高文淑和她的丈夫均被非法庭审，当庭未予宣判。之后，高文淑的家人为她聘请了律师，但律师向法官提出再次庭审要求时遭到拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其夫妇二人被山东青岛城阳区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别宣判，其被重判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，其丈夫被重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。两人不服，均已提出上诉。目前被关押在青岛市城阳看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、杭霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">合肥法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日杭霞被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月开庭未判。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，合肥瑶海区法院近期到看守所向杭霞单独宣判：判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。不准上诉。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、何华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贵阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">55</span>岁的何华女士，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日向路人发送<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年新年挂历，被巡逻特警抓捕，先被关押在贵阳市云岩区拘留所，后转到贵阳市云岩区看守所。先判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，后检察院抗诉，又于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日贵阳市中级法院又改判何华<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、侯巧珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北邯郸市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年已七十七岁，是邯郸市一位退休教师。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下午，侯巧珍与张培英在邯郸市复兴区彭家寨附近讲述法轮功被迫害真相时，被告发，遭复兴区公安分局彭家寨派出所抓捕，被关押在邯郸市第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，邯郸市磁县法院在邯郸第三看守所里暗箱操作，对侯巧珍和张培英开庭，后判侯巧珍<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑，张培英<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。侯巧珍刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">9</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、蒋立宇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">原在北京一家教育机构工作。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日晚上，她和法轮功学员田丰及单珊，在北京街头张贴揭露“天安门自焚假案”的不干胶贴纸，被非法抓捕关押至今。据大陆媒体报导，蒋立宇、田丰及单珊分别被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">10</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、鞠小林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆维权人士刘富祥的朋友。刘富祥位于重庆市九龙坡区石桥铺正街<span lang="EN-US">202</span>号房屋，因为拆迁问题未与地方政府达成拆迁协议。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，刘富祥和儿子刘汗、侄女刘丽珺、朋友鞠小林在家中休息，被一群不明身份人闯入，将四人打伤打残，刘富祥和儿子刘汗全身多处骨折。随后四人被以妨碍公务罪抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午，刘富祥妨碍公务案开庭宣判，到法庭旁听出来的刘富祥的姐姐刘富兰哭诉：弟弟刘富祥被重判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、侄儿刘汗被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、侄女刘丽珺被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">22</span>天、鞠小林被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。鞠小林刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">11</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、李瑞华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因谢万猛在深圳市粘贴法轮大法真相不干胶被监控追踪至出租房。当时，在谢万猛家中有法轮功学员吴锐及从北京过去看吴锐的李瑞华，他们也同时被罗湖区警察抓捕。谢万猛被罗湖区警察上门抄家、抓捕，警察抢走<span lang="EN-US">10000</span>左右现金、电脑、手机等私人物品。谢万猛、吴锐、李瑞华（女）、于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被非法开庭，未当庭宣判。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日上午十一点半左右，深圳市盐田区法院宣判结果。吴锐、李瑞华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年并罚金<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元，谢万猛被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">12</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、李天学：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市金州区石河镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚，谷秀华（女）、刘希永（男）、周兴（男）、李天学（男）、王丽志（女）、张三曼（女）、谭春荣（女）、孙宝英（女）、刘井龙（男），去大连市金普新区炮台镇袁屯村发放新书《共产主义的终极目的》，被炮台镇派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午二在大连市金州法院庭审。后谷秀华、周兴、王丽志，被大连市金州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；张三曼、谭春荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，李天学被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刘希永、孙宝英、刘井龙的情况还不清楚。李天学刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">13</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、李媛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，辽宁省沈阳市人，辽阳市朝光村基督教家庭教会骨干成员，中国在押良心犯。因其教会为基督教家庭教会，且不愿到中共当局指定的“三自”教会敬拜、聚会，遂遭致当局的严打惩罚；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其被辽阳市太子河区警方突然抓捕刑拘，并被指控教会内部使用了基督徒信仰灵修崇拜书籍及相关印刷品，并在教会的便利店销往其他省市，属于非法买卖行为；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被辽宁省辽阳市太子河区法院以“非法经营罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。目前被羁押于辽阳市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">14</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、刘美廷：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西运城访民刘美廷与韩丽芳夫妇于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被警方刑事拘留，警方指控他们于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月在微信群发布大量令中共当局不满的信息，这是典型的因言治罪。刘美廷与韩丽芳夫妇于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被运城法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年与<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">刘美廷刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日</b>，韩丽芳刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。 后两人上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，山西省高院撤销了原判决，要求运城市中院重新审理，后续进展未知。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">15</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、马月琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省漯河市临颖县退休女教师、法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人。马月琴<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日去临颖县杜曲镇面对面发法轮功台历时被抓捕，关押在漯河市第二看守所，经查证，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7-8</span>月间被临颖法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">16</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、牛占华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">沈阳市法库县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日<span lang="EN-US">0</span>时许，秀水河子镇派出所警察没有法定手续，擅自闯入牛占华家，翻箱倒柜，非法搜查，还带走牛占华和在牛占华家做客的周建国。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，牛占华在辽宁省沈阳市法库县法院被庭审。整个庭审现场被律师有理有据的辩护所主导，法官与公诉人大部份时间是听律师在讲，公诉人只是照本宣科的读了《起诉书》。最后律师要求法院应当立即释放牛占华。后于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月对他判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">17</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、冉文芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">成都青年法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，钟华、冉文芳在街上给一个人讲了大法真相，当她们离开后，这个人拨打<span lang="EN-US">110</span>恶意举报，驷马桥派出所通过监控，找到正在回家路上的钟华和冉文芳，将她们抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，钟华和冉文芳被成都金牛区法院判刑，钟华<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万，冉文芳<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金六千元。她们上诉后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，成都市中院法院对她们维持原判。钟华和冉文芳被非法关押在成都郫县看守所，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">18</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、单珊：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日晚上，单珊和法轮功学员田丰及蒋立宇，在北京街头张贴揭露“天安门自焚假案”的不干胶贴纸，被非法抓捕关押至今。据大陆媒体报导，蒋立宇、田丰及单珊分别被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">19</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、王文卿：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宁夏访民。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年，王文卿经多方筹措借款<span lang="EN-US">54</span>万元，购买了一辆斯太尔重型运输车，挂靠在一家运输公司跑运输，结果被宁夏回族自治区银川市兴庆区法院扣押，公司经理传话，说法官为要五条软中华香烟，再请客吃顿饭，就可以将车辆拿回来了。由于王文卿坚信法院的扣押行为违法，法官不敢怎么地，就没有理会，结果车辆最终被拍卖。到<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，王文卿的妻子吴爱珍因身体不适，到医院检查发现已罹患癌症。维权十多年的王文卿此时已家徒四壁，就于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日上午，到石嘴山市惠农区政府找区领导，要求给予政策规定的大病救助，结果保安以领导开会为由，打电话通知南街派出所，以“扰乱单位工作秩序、及谩骂党和国家干部”为由，将王文卿强制传唤到派出所。后公安局就以“涉嫌妨害公务罪”对王文卿拘留、批捕、公诉，在一审开庭审理之际，王文卿的妻子悲愤交加下撒手人寰！惠农区法院依旧对王文卿作出“妨害公务罪”成立刑事判决，判刑六个月，缓期执行一年。 刑事判决炮制出笼后，王文卿继续上访维权。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，当局为了遏制王文卿的上访行动，要求王文卿补签认罪认罚书，但王文卿坚决予以拒绝，当局才以王文卿拒绝接受社区矫正为由，撤销缓期执行的判决，对其再收监。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">20</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、吴锐：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因谢万猛在深圳市粘贴法轮大法真相不干胶被监控追踪至出租房。当时，在谢万猛家中有法轮功学员吴锐及从北京过去看吴锐的李瑞华，他们也同时被罗湖区警察抓捕。谢万猛被罗湖区警察上门抄家、抓捕，警察抢走<span lang="EN-US">10000</span>左右现金、电脑、手机等私人物品。谢万猛、吴锐、李瑞华（女）、于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被非法开庭，未当庭宣判。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日上午十一点半左右，深圳市盐田区法院宣判结果。吴锐、李瑞华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年并罚金<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元，谢万猛被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">21</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、扎西加：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日生，果洛州玛沁县牧民，被捕前居住于玛沁县拉加镇黄河小区。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日因涉嫌“煽动分裂国家罪”被拘留，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被逮捕。当局指控 扎西加通过网络下载涉藏非法图片和视频，于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，通过微信向朋友转发<span lang="EN-US">14</span>世达赖喇嘛讲经照片<span lang="EN-US">4</span>张。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，扎西加在个人微信朋友圈内发布一张含有雪山狮子旗和洛桑孙根<span lang="EN-US">(</span>即洛桑森格，藏人行政中央司政<span lang="EN-US">)</span>照片，获得其微信朋友的点赞和评论。同年，扎西加在被视为“三月敏感期”的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，通过微信对朋友转发被指控含有“藏独”内容的“新年祝辞视频”。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，扎西加向微信群转发“期盼十四世达赖喇嘛返藏”，与“含有达赖喇嘛和洛桑孙根内容”的图片和短视频。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，当局突然将扎西加传唤到派出所接受调查，当时，当局对扎西加的行政处罚是行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，而<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，当局决定对扎西加延长拘留时间，至<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日正式决定予以批捕。当局请求西藏自治区新闻出版局和西藏自治区质量检测中心鉴定扎西加所发的图片视频，经鉴定，扎西加的图片和视频含有“危害国家主权，安全和领土完整”内容。果洛州检察院对扎西加提起公诉后，果洛州中级法院在审理期间，没有公开审理此案，对其做出秘密审判。扎西加受审时辩解称“图片和视频被浏览，转发量很少”，法院认为与事实不符，予以驳回。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，青海果洛州玛沁县牧民扎西加因“煽动分裂国家罪”被果洛州中级法院判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">22</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、战玉彩：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年三十二岁的女研究生、济南法轮功学员。在中共对法轮功持续至今近二十年的迫害中，战玉彩女士第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被判刑。她在<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被济南历下区法院判刑四年；随后她丈夫杜泽洲被济南长清区警察跟踪抓捕，被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，至今仍在山东省监狱关押迫害。战玉彩女士<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚九点左右，从济南历下区姚家庄去往政法学院的路上张贴真相不干胶时，当场被后面跟踪的济南历下区智远派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，战玉彩被抓捕到济南市看守所非法关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被济南市历下区法院开庭，被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">23</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、赵春侠</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，辽宁省辽阳市人，基督徒，辽阳市朝光村基督教家庭教会会计。因其教会为基督教家庭教会，且不愿到中共当局指定的“三自”教会敬拜、聚会，遂遭致当局的严打惩罚；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其被辽阳市太子河区警方突然抓捕刑拘，并被指控教会内部使用了基督徒信仰灵修崇拜书籍及相关印刷品，并在教会的便利店销往其他省市，属于非法买卖行为；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被辽宁省辽阳市太子河区法院以“非法经营罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。目前被羁押于辽阳市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">24</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、赵广军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">维权老兵。户籍地是辽宁省盘锦市兴隆台区；他的出生地是黑龙江省望奎县；他当兵在锦州四十军<span lang="EN-US">81056</span>部队；他原工作单位是<span lang="EN-US">(</span>北京<span lang="EN-US">)</span>中石油长城钻探；他多年住北京上访；他被维稳的责任单位是兴隆台区。赵广军走上公民维权之路后，因参与公民维权活动、关注侵犯个案，十数次被关黑监狱，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被行政拘留，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>次被刑事拘留，两次被构陷入狱。近一年以来，赵广军多次遭到绑架、软禁，曾经在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月开始的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月中，相继<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次被限制人身自由。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，赵广军在北京被盘锦警方抓走以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，关押在盘锦市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日赵广军被正式批捕，目前家人已经收到逮捕通知书。赵广军此次被抓捕完全是因言获罪。赵广军于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 11</span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 27</span>日 被盘锦市兴隆台区法院判处寻衅滋事罪，获刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">25</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、赵桂春</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：内蒙古赤峰元宝山区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生。十九年来，在中共对法轮功学员的血腥迫害中，她受尽了苦难。赵桂春曾经在内蒙古图牧吉劳教所被非法监禁<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，遭惨无人道的折磨；流离失所<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月和<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月两次被劫持到赤峰喀喇沁旗看守所关押，绝食抗议迫害一个多月后，出现极其危险的症状，保外就医，被迫流离失所。被通缉<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被抓捕，赵桂春获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，随后被关押到内蒙古女子监狱。内蒙古女子监狱每次都阻挠亲人会见。监狱中遭受殴打虐待。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">26</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、朱纯荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江鸡西市鸡冠区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，鸡西市鸡冠区十名法轮功学员遭黑龙江省公安、鸡西市警察绑架，其中法轮功学员朱纯荣，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被哈尔滨道里区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">27</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、毛坤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川成都市金牛区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日下午，杜荣、张珍华、陈世贵正在友人毛坤家做客休息，被成都市金牛区分局国保警察、茶店子派出所孟红等一伙警察疯狂砸门抓捕。毛坤当场被毒打致使手臂骨折<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，毛坤、杜荣、张珍华、陈世贵被四川省成都市金牛区法院判刑，判刑毛坤<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年半，罚款两万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。二零二一年四月十一日被迫害致死。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
